font-weight: bold;">Mischmasch</span>! </p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kadét</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́тов</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́т</a></strong></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадетский.html>каде́тский</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">meaning "cadet"</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><br />
<strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kadét</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадет.html>каде́тов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадетский.html>каде́тский</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">meaning "Constitutional Democrat"</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кадило.html>кади́ло</a> (30349)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Kadilo_pskov.jpg/220px-Kadilo_pskov.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="401" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Kadilo_pskov.jpg/330px-Kadilo_pskov.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/Kadilo_pskov.jpg/440px-Kadilo_pskov.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1556" data-file-height="2836" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:кадило.html>кади́ло</a></div></div></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадило.html>кади́ло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kadilo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">incense</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kadidlo</i>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">кади́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ло</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>

<p><b>ка<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ди.html>ди́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ло</b>

Зализняка).

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадр.html>ка́дры</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kádry</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровый.html>ка́дровый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kádrovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> personnel, human resources
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровый.html>ка́дровая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:политика.html>поли́тика</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kádrovaja</b> polítika</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>personnel/staffing</b> policy</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cadre
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровый.html>ка́дровый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:состав.html>соста́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kádrovyj</b> sostáv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the <b>cadre</b></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>cadre</b> staff</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровый.html>ка́дровый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kádrovyj</b> rabóčij</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>cadre</b> worker</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровый.html>ка́дровый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дипломат.html>диплома́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kádrovyj</b> diplomát</i> ― <span class="e-translation">career diplomat</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>cadre</b> diplomat</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> regular
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровый.html>ка́дровый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:офицер.html>офице́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kádrovyj</b> oficér</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>regular</b> officer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> frame
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кадровый.html>ка́дровая</a></b> развёртка</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kádrovaja</b> razvjórtka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>frame</b> deflection/scan</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***казак.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>казак</a> (3872)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">козак</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kozak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> languages ("free, independent person, an adventurer, a drifter"), cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казах.html>каза́х</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazáx</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Kazakh</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>каза́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kazák</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>казака́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>казаки́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>каза́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>казако́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>каза́ков</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казачок.html>каза́чка</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Cossack, cossack</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:казарменный.html>каза́рменный</a> (18511)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казарма.html>каза́рма</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazárma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казарменный.html>каза́рменный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kazármennyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> barracks</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rude, vulgar, pejorative</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:казать.html>каза́ть</a> (20478)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kāzàti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казать.html>каза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kazátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выказать.html>вы́казать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to show</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tell</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to indicate</li></ol>

<p><b>ка<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>за́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 6c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:показать.html>показа́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:указать.html>указа́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-каз-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>. <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>
</p>

***казаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>каза́ться</a> (142)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казать.html>каза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>каза́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kazátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:показаться.html>показа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to seem, to appear, to look
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>ка́жется</a>, (<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> где́-то <a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́дел</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne kážetsja, (što) ja jevó gdé-to vídel.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It seems to me (i.e. I think) I saw him somewhere.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ка<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>за́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 6c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:показаться.html>показа́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>Фо́рма</a> ед.ч. <a href = vnd.unilang:повести.html>повёл</a>. накл. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>кажи́сь</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>употребля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просторечие.html>просторе́чии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:качество.html>ка́честве</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вводный.html>вво́дного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова</a>.
<a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>Фо́рма</a> 3 л. ед.ч. <a href = vnd.unilang:наст.html>наст</a>. вр. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>ка́жется</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>употребля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:качество.html>ка́честве</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вводный.html>вво́дного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:частица.html>части́цы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> предикатива.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-каз-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***казах.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:казах.html>каза́х</a> (9605)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">казахста́н</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Kazaxstán</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:казачий.html>каза́чий</a></b>
</p><p>Притяжательное <a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — местоименное <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> 6*a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-казач-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ий</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>каза́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazák</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казачок.html>казачо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kazačók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казачок.html>казачка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казачок.html>казачки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казачок.html>казачко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>kazachok, kozachok <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">dance</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">endearing diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>каза́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazák</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (young, little) Cossack <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">can also be condescending</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> boy servant</li></ol>
